# 轻小说 2022 NPM、PYPI、DockerHub 备份

## 爱的成人式 - 干胡桃 - 20221205


### Docker

```
docker pull apachecn0/ai-de-chengrenshi-gan-hutao-20221205
docker run -tid -p <port>:80 apachecn0/ai-de-chengrenshi-gan-hutao-20221205
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### PYPI

```
pip install ai-de-chengrenshi-gan-hutao-20221205
ai-de-chengrenshi-gan-hutao-20221205 <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### NPM

```
npm install -g ai-de-chengrenshi-gan-hutao-erlingereryierlingwu
ai-de-chengrenshi-gan-hutao-erlingereryierlingwu <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```
